posted:Posted May 2, 2022
msg:I stayed from April 30 to May 2,2022.  The room and the view was beautiful and clean.  I enjoyed the bathtub and took advantage of it so many times.  I was pleasantly surprised by the service in the executive lounge. They were so friendly and accommodating.  One attendant I enjoyed speaking with quite a bit. Another attendant arranged to have someone escort me to covid-testing place so I could get it done for free.  The service in the restaurant on May 1st was outstanding. Because of COVID restrictions, service was limited to ordering.  But the waitress was so accomodating. She arranged a set of pastries for me. She brought me juice. She brought me two sets of pancakes because they were so small, and buffet style i would have had more than what was given.  She was always available.  And it made me feel valued. I really appreciated the service and I was looking forward to breakfast the next day.  However, this standard of service was not to be repeated.  On May 2, I went down and there were only three of us in the restaurant, a Chinese couple and myself.   The waitress seemed very unwilling to serve me.  I noticed the other table was full of food.  I had ordered two sets of pancakes and only received one (each serving had two very small pancakes on it).  She brought about a plate of pastries but interrupted me when I wanted to choose more than one pastry and said wait a moment. Then she went over to the other table and had them order. She never brought back the pastries again.  She never offered to serve me any more food after that. She brought the other table several coffees but I was not offered the opportunity to order any more.  She acted busy but was doing nothing and I felt so humiliated.  I know that I am not Chinese. But it is a hotel, and there were only three of us in the restaurant. The contrast to the service the day before was so opposite.  Both tables are guests. We both should have had the same service.  If it had been busy, I would have been more understanding.

msg:Although this stay was short, it left a very deep impression on me, and I must talk about it!
Service: The overall quality of the hotel staff is very high. The impression given from the moment I entered the door was very good. The young lady generously and enthusiastically led me to the front desk, and the front desk was able to solve all the problems I raised with care. The sister who cleaned my room was very considerate and would help me sort out the messy items and scattered clothes. The concierge was even more considerate to help me plan the travel route.
Environment: Although the hotel is located near the Third Ring Road, it does not feel noisy at all. It overlooks the city landscape and gets warm and quiet in the hustle and bustle. The rooms and restaurants are spacious and bright, and the beds are also very comfortable, allowing me to enjoy a good sleep.
Breakfast: This must be emphasized. Their breakfast restaurant has its own style. It is called the library restaurant. All the food is on the bookshelf, elegant and unique.
Facilities: Although the hotel has been open for more than 10 years, it is still very well maintained, and it is more reassuring to live without formaldehyde.
To sum up, if I come to Beijing next time, I am afraid that the only choice is the Conrad Hotel Beijing.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:During the May Day trip to Beijing, I stayed at Conrad. The main building was designed by Ma Yansong, which is quite iconic for a hotel.
Transportation: It is close to the Third Ring Road, so it is very convenient to take a taxi or the subway. It takes about half an hour to get from Beijing South Railway Station to the hotel by subway.
Environment: Next to it is Tuanjiehu Park, where you can overlook the pleasure of boating on the lake in the park. The hotel is not far from the Guomao business district and the Sanlitun business district, about a 20-minute walk. If you don't like crowded and noisy places, Conrad, which is hidden in the city, must be suitable for you.
Facilities and hygiene: The hotel has been open for more than ten years, and the facilities and home maintenance are OK. The overall decoration style and room layout are more in line with my expectations. The library breakfast restaurant on the first floor is a holy place to open, and it is easy to take pictures. The view of the executive lounge is great (I didn't go to the top floor because I upgraded to a panoramic room this time)

The concierge offered to deliver the luggage to the room after the room was cleaned (very considerate). The cleaning lady was very polite and helped me fold my pajamas during the cleaning (a bit unexpected).
Finally, a little digression: Conrad's panoramic room is worth recommending, the view is great (even more amazing when the China Zun is lit at night); I think Conrad is also a perfect match for those who want to eat Four Seasons Minfu roast duck.
